49/* Test that g_unichar_type() returns the correct value for various
50 * ASCII and Unicode alphabetic, numeric, and other, codepoints. */
51static void
52test_unichar_character_type (void)
53{
54 guint i;
55 struct {
56 GUnicodeType type;
57 gunichar c;
58 } examples[] = {
59 { G_UNICODE_CONTROL, 0x000D },
60 { G_UNICODE_FORMAT, 0x200E },
61 /* G_UNICODE_UNASSIGNED */
62 { G_UNICODE_PRIVATE_USE, 0xE000 },
63 { G_UNICODE_SURROGATE, 0xD800 },
64 { G_UNICODE_LOWERCASE_LETTER, 0x0061 },
65 { G_UNICODE_MODIFIER_LETTER, 0x02B0 },
66 { G_UNICODE_OTHER_LETTER, 0x3400 },
67 { G_UNICODE_TITLECASE_LETTER, 0x01C5 },
68 { G_UNICODE_UPPERCASE_LETTER, 0xFF21 },
69 { G_UNICODE_SPACING_MARK, 0x0903 },
70 { G_UNICODE_ENCLOSING_MARK, 0x20DD },
71 { G_UNICODE_NON_SPACING_MARK, 0xA806 },
72 { G_UNICODE_DECIMAL_NUMBER, 0xFF10 },
73 { G_UNICODE_LETTER_NUMBER, 0x16EE },
74 { G_UNICODE_OTHER_NUMBER, 0x17F0 },
75 { G_UNICODE_CONNECT_PUNCTUATION, 0x005F },
76 { G_UNICODE_DASH_PUNCTUATION, 0x058A },
77 { G_UNICODE_CLOSE_PUNCTUATION, 0x0F3B },
78 { G_UNICODE_FINAL_PUNCTUATION, 0x2019 },
79 { G_UNICODE_INITIAL_PUNCTUATION, 0x2018 },
80 { G_UNICODE_OTHER_PUNCTUATION, 0x2016 },
81 { G_UNICODE_OPEN_PUNCTUATION, 0x0F3A },
82 { G_UNICODE_CURRENCY_SYMBOL, 0x20A0 },
83 { G_UNICODE_MODIFIER_SYMBOL, 0x309B },
84 { G_UNICODE_MATH_SYMBOL, 0xFB29 },
85 { G_UNICODE_OTHER_SYMBOL, 0x00A6 },
86 { G_UNICODE_LINE_SEPARATOR, 0x2028 },
87 { G_UNICODE_PARAGRAPH_SEPARATOR, 0x2029 },
88 { G_UNICODE_SPACE_SEPARATOR, 0x202F },
89 };
90
91 for (i = 0; i < G_N_ELEMENTS (examples)(sizeof (examples) / sizeof ((examples)[0])); i++)
92 {
93 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_type (examples[i].c), ==, examples[i].type)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_type (examples[i].c)), __n2 = (
examples[i].type); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum
("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 93, ((const char*) (__func__
)), "g_unichar_type (examples[i].c)" " " "==" " " "examples[i].type"
, (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while
(0);
94 }
95
96 /*** Testing TYPE() border cases ***/
97 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_type (0x3FF5), ==, 0x07)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_type (0x3FF5)), __n2 = (0x07); if
(__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c"
, 97, ((const char*) (__func__)), "g_unichar_type (0x3FF5)" " "
"==" " " "0x07", (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2
, 'i'); } while (0);
98 /* U+FFEFF Plane 15 Private Use */
99 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_type (0xFFEFF), ==, 0x03)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_type (0xFFEFF)), __n2 = (0x03);
if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib",
"../glib/tests/unicode.c", 99, ((const char*) (__func__)), "g_unichar_type (0xFFEFF)"
" " "==" " " "0x03", (long double) __n1, "==", (long double)
__n2, 'i'); } while (0);
100 /* U+E0001 Language Tag */
101 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_type (0xE0001), ==, 0x01)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_type (0xE0001)), __n2 = (0x01);
if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib",
"../glib/tests/unicode.c", 101, ((const char*) (__func__)), "g_unichar_type (0xE0001)"
" " "==" " " "0x01", (long double) __n1, "==", (long double)
__n2, 'i'); } while (0);
102 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_type (G_UNICODE_LAST_CHAR), ==, 0x02)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_type (0x10ffff)), __n2 = (0x02)
; if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib"
, "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 102, ((const char*) (__func__)),
"g_unichar_type (G_UNICODE_LAST_CHAR)" " " "==" " " "0x02", (
long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0
);
103 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_type (G_UNICODE_LAST_CHAR + 1), ==, 0x02)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_type (0x10ffff + 1)), __n2 = (0x02
); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib"
, "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 103, ((const char*) (__func__)),
"g_unichar_type (G_UNICODE_LAST_CHAR + 1)" " " "==" " " "0x02"
, (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while
(0);
104 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_type (G_UNICODE_LAST_CHAR_PART1), ==, 0x02)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_type (0x313FF)), __n2 = (0x02);
if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib",
"../glib/tests/unicode.c", 104, ((const char*) (__func__)), "g_unichar_type (G_UNICODE_LAST_CHAR_PART1)"
" " "==" " " "0x02", (long double) __n1, "==", (long double)
__n2, 'i'); } while (0);
105 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_type (G_UNICODE_LAST_CHAR_PART1 + 1), ==, 0x02)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_type (0x313FF + 1)), __n2 = (0x02
); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib"
, "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 105, ((const char*) (__func__)),
"g_unichar_type (G_UNICODE_LAST_CHAR_PART1 + 1)" " " "==" " "
"0x02", (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); }
while (0);
106}

371 { 21, 0x05BC },
372 { 22, 0x05BD },
373 { 23, 0x05BF },
374 { 24, 0x05C1 },
375 { 25, 0x05C2 },
376 { 26, 0xFB1E },
377 { 27, 0x064B },
378 { 28, 0x064C },
379 { 29, 0x064D },
380 /* ... */
381 { 228, 0x05AE },
382 { 230, 0x0300 },
383 { 232, 0x302C },
384 { 233, 0x0362 },
385 { 234, 0x0360 },
386 { 234, 0x1DCD },
387 { 240, 0x0345 }
388 };
389 for (i = 0; i < G_N_ELEMENTS (examples)(sizeof (examples) / sizeof ((examples)[0])); i++)
390 {
391 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_combining_class (examples[i].c), ==, examples[i].class)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_combining_class (examples[i].c)

, (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while
(0);

417/* Test that g_utf8_strup() returns the correct value for various
418 * ASCII and Unicode alphabetic, numeric, and other, codepoints. */
419static void
420test_strup (void)
421{
422 char *str_up = NULL((void*)0);
423 const char *str = "AaZz09x;\x03\x45"
424 "\xEF\xBD\x81" /* Unichar 'A' (U+FF21) */
425 "\xEF\xBC\xA1"; /* Unichar 'a' (U+FF41) */
426
427 /* Testing degenerated cases */
428 if (g_test_undefined ()(g_test_config_vars->test_undefined))
429 {
430 g_test_expect_message (G_LOG_DOMAIN"GLib", G_LOG_LEVEL_CRITICAL,
431 "*assertion*!= NULL*");
432 str_up = g_utf8_strup (NULL((void*)0), 0);
Value stored to 'str_up' is never read
433 g_test_assert_expected_messages ()g_test_assert_expected_messages_internal ("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c"
, 433, ((const char*) (__func__)));
434 }
435
436 str_up = g_utf8_strup (str, strlen (str));
437 /* Tricky, comparing two unicode strings with an ASCII function */
438 g_assert_cmpstr (str_up, ==, "AAZZ09X;\003E\357\274\241\357\274\241")do { const char *__s1 = (str_up), *__s2 = ("AAZZ09X;\003E\357\274\241\357\274\241"
); if (g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr
("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 438, ((const char*) (__func__
)), "str_up" " " "==" " " "\"AAZZ09X;\\003E\\357\\274\\241\\357\\274\\241\""
, __s1, "==", __s2); } while (0);
439 g_free (str_up);
440}

)), "'" "g_unichar_ismark (0xFFEFF)" "' should be FALSE"); } while
(0);

; if (!(g_unichar_ismark (0xE0001))) _g_boolean_var_ = 1; else
_g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else g_assertion_message

; if (!(g_unichar_ismark (0x10ffff))) _g_boolean_var_ = 1; else

("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 508, ((const char*) (__func__

642/* Test that g_unichar_digit_value() returns the correct value for various
643 * ASCII and Unicode alphabetic, numeric, and other, codepoints. */
644static void
645test_digit_value (void)
646{
647 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_digit_value (' '), ==, -1)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_digit_value (' ')), __n2 = (-1)
; if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib"
, "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 647, ((const char*) (__func__)),
"g_unichar_digit_value (' ')" " " "==" " " "-1", (long double
) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0);
648 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_digit_value ('a'), ==, -1)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_digit_value ('a')), __n2 = (-1)
; if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib"
, "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 648, ((const char*) (__func__)),
"g_unichar_digit_value ('a')" " " "==" " " "-1", (long double
) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0);
649 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_digit_value ('0'), ==, 0)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_digit_value ('0')), __n2 = (0);
if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib",
"../glib/tests/unicode.c", 649, ((const char*) (__func__)), "g_unichar_digit_value ('0')"
" " "==" " " "0", (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2
, 'i'); } while (0);
650 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_digit_value ('9'), ==, 9)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_digit_value ('9')), __n2 = (9);
if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib",
"../glib/tests/unicode.c", 650, ((const char*) (__func__)), "g_unichar_digit_value ('9')"
" " "==" " " "9", (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2
, 'i'); } while (0);
651 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_digit_value ('A'), ==, -1)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_digit_value ('A')), __n2 = (-1)
; if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib"
, "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 651, ((const char*) (__func__)),
"g_unichar_digit_value ('A')" " " "==" " " "-1", (long double
) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0);
652 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_digit_value ('-'), ==, -1)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_digit_value ('-')), __n2 = (-1)
; if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib"
, "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 652, ((const char*) (__func__)),
"g_unichar_digit_value ('-')" " " "==" " " "-1", (long double
) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0);
653 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_digit_value (0xFF21), ==, -1)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_digit_value (0xFF21)), __n2 = (
-1); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib"
, "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 653, ((const char*) (__func__)),
"g_unichar_digit_value (0xFF21)" " " "==" " " "-1", (long double
) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0); /* Unichar 'A' */
654 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_digit_value (0xFF3A), ==, -1)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_digit_value (0xFF3A)), __n2 = (
-1); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib"

715/* Test that g_unichar_xdigit_value() returns the correct value for various
716 * ASCII and Unicode alphabetic, numeric, and other, codepoints. */
717static void
718test_xdigit_value (void)
719{
720 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_xdigit_value (' '), ==, -1)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_xdigit_value (' ')), __n2 = (-1
); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib"
, "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 720, ((const char*) (__func__)),
"g_unichar_xdigit_value (' ')" " " "==" " " "-1", (long double
) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0);
721 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_xdigit_value ('a'), ==, 10)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_xdigit_value ('a')), __n2 = (10
); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib"
, "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 721, ((const char*) (__func__)),
"g_unichar_xdigit_value ('a')" " " "==" " " "10", (long double
) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0);
722 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_xdigit_value ('f'), ==, 15)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_xdigit_value ('f')), __n2 = (15
); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib"
, "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 722, ((const char*) (__func__)),

989/* Test that g_unichar_toupper() and g_unichar_tolower() return the
990 * correct values for various ASCII and Unicode alphabetic, numeric,
991 * and other, codepoints. */
992static void
993test_cases (void)
994{
995 g_assert_cmphex (g_unichar_toupper (0x0), ==, 0x0)do { guint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_toupper (0x0)), __n2 = (0x0); if
(__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c"
, 995, ((const char*) (__func__)), "g_unichar_toupper (0x0)" " "
"==" " " "0x0", (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2
, 'x'); } while (0);
996 g_assert_cmphex (g_unichar_tolower (0x0), ==, 0x0)do { guint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_tolower (0x0)), __n2 = (0x0); if
(__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c"
, 996, ((const char*) (__func__)), "g_unichar_tolower (0x0)" " "
"==" " " "0x0", (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2
, 'x'); } while (0);
997 g_assert_cmphex (g_unichar_toupper ('a'), ==, 'A')do { guint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_toupper ('a')), __n2 = ('A'); if
(__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c"
, 997, ((const char*) (__func__)), "g_unichar_toupper ('a')" " "
"==" " " "'A'", (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2
, 'x'); } while (0);
998 g_assert_cmphex (g_unichar_toupper ('A'), ==, 'A')do { guint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_toupper ('A')), __n2 = ('A'); if
(__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c"
, 998, ((const char*) (__func__)), "g_unichar_toupper ('A')" " "
"==" " " "'A'", (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2
, 'x'); } while (0);
999 /* Unicode fullwidth 'a' == 'A' */

1065{

_g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else g_assertion_message

1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else

1086
1087/* Test that g_unichar_iswide() returns the correct value for various
1088 * ASCII and Unicode alphabetic, numeric, and other, codepoints. */
1089static void
1090test_wide (void)
1091{
1092 guint i;
1093 struct {
1094 gunichar c;
1095 enum {
1096 NOT_WIDE,
1097 WIDE_CJK,
1098 WIDE
1099 } wide;
1100 } examples[] = {
1101 /* Neutral */
1102 { 0x0000, NOT_WIDE },
1103 { 0x0483, NOT_WIDE },
1104 { 0x0641, NOT_WIDE },
1105 { 0xFFFC, NOT_WIDE },
1106 { 0x10000, NOT_WIDE },
1107 { 0xE0001, NOT_WIDE },
1108 { 0x2FFFE, NOT_WIDE },
1109 { 0x3FFFE, NOT_WIDE },
1110
1111 /* Narrow */
1112 { 0x0020, NOT_WIDE },
1113 { 0x0041, NOT_WIDE },
1114 { 0x27E6, NOT_WIDE },
1115
1116 /* Halfwidth */
1117 { 0x20A9, NOT_WIDE },
1118 { 0xFF61, NOT_WIDE },
1119 { 0xFF69, NOT_WIDE },
1120 { 0xFFEE, NOT_WIDE },
1121
1122 /* Ambiguous */
1123 { 0x00A1, WIDE_CJK },
1124 { 0x00BE, WIDE_CJK },
1125 { 0x02DD, WIDE_CJK },
1126 { 0x2020, WIDE_CJK },
1127 { 0xFFFD, WIDE_CJK },
1128 { 0x00A1, WIDE_CJK },
1129 { 0x1F100, WIDE_CJK },
1130 { 0xE0100, WIDE_CJK },
1131 { 0x100000, WIDE_CJK },
1132 { 0x10FFFD, WIDE_CJK },
1133
1134 /* Fullwidth */
1135 { 0x3000, WIDE },
1136 { 0xFF60, WIDE },
1137
1138 /* Wide */
1139 { 0x2329, WIDE },
1140 { 0x3001, WIDE },
1141 { 0xFE69, WIDE },
1142 { 0x30000, WIDE },
1143 { 0x3FFFD, WIDE },
1144
1145 /* Default Wide blocks */
1146 { 0x4DBF, WIDE },
1147 { 0x9FFF, WIDE },
1148 { 0xFAFF, WIDE },
1149 { 0x2A6DF, WIDE },
1150 { 0x2B73F, WIDE },
1151 { 0x2B81F, WIDE },
1152 { 0x2FA1F, WIDE },
1153
1154 /* Uniode-5.2 character additions */
1155 /* Wide */
1156 { 0x115F, WIDE },
1157
1158 /* Uniode-6.0 character additions */
1159 /* Wide */
1160 { 0x2B740, WIDE },
1161 { 0x1B000, WIDE },
1162
1163 { 0x111111, NOT_WIDE }
1164 };
1165
1166 for (i = 0; i < G_N_ELEMENTS (examples)(sizeof (examples) / sizeof ((examples)[0])); i++)
1167 {
1168 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_iswide (examples[i].c), ==,do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_iswide (examples[i].c)), __n2 =
((examples[i].wide == WIDE)); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum
("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 1169, ((const char*) (__func__
)), "g_unichar_iswide (examples[i].c)" " " "==" " " "(examples[i].wide == WIDE)"
, (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while
(0)
1169 (examples[i].wide == WIDE))do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_iswide (examples[i].c)), __n2 =
((examples[i].wide == WIDE)); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum
("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 1169, ((const char*) (__func__
)), "g_unichar_iswide (examples[i].c)" " " "==" " " "(examples[i].wide == WIDE)"
, (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while
(0);
1170 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_iswide_cjk (examples[i].c), ==,do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_iswide_cjk (examples[i].c)), __n2
= ((examples[i].wide != NOT_WIDE)); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else
g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c"
, 1171, ((const char*) (__func__)), "g_unichar_iswide_cjk (examples[i].c)"
" " "==" " " "(examples[i].wide != NOT_WIDE)", (long double)
__n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0)
1171 (examples[i].wide != NOT_WIDE))do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_iswide_cjk (examples[i].c)), __n2
= ((examples[i].wide != NOT_WIDE)); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else
g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c"
, 1171, ((const char*) (__func__)), "g_unichar_iswide_cjk (examples[i].c)"
" " "==" " " "(examples[i].wide != NOT_WIDE)", (long double)
__n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0);
1172 }
1173};

1246/* Test that g_unichar_fully_decompose() returns the correct value for
1247 * various ASCII and Unicode alphabetic, numeric, and other, codepoints. */
1248static void
1249test_fully_decompose_canonical (void)
1250{
1251 gunichar decomp[5];
1252 gsize len;
1253
1254#define TEST_DECOMP(ch, expected_len, a, b, c, d) \
1255 len = g_unichar_fully_decompose (ch, FALSE(0), decomp, G_N_ELEMENTS (decomp)(sizeof (decomp) / sizeof ((decomp)[0]))); \
1256 g_assert_cmpint (expected_len, ==, len)do { gint64 __n1 = (expected_len), __n2 = (len); if (__n1 == __n2
) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c"
, 1256, ((const char*) (__func__)), "expected_len" " " "==" " "
"len", (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); }
while (0); \
1257 if (expected_len >= 1) g_assert_cmphex (decomp[0], ==, a)do { guint64 __n1 = (decomp[0]), __n2 = (a); if (__n1 == __n2
) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c"
, 1257, ((const char*) (__func__)), "decomp[0]" " " "==" " " "a"
, (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'x'); } while
(0); \
1258 if (expected_len >= 2) g_assert_cmphex (decomp[1], ==, b)do { guint64 __n1 = (decomp[1]), __n2 = (b); if (__n1 == __n2
) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c"
, 1258, ((const char*) (__func__)), "decomp[1]" " " "==" " " "b"
, (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'x'); } while
(0); \
1259 if (expected_len >= 3) g_assert_cmphex (decomp[2], ==, c)do { guint64 __n1 = (decomp[2]), __n2 = (c); if (__n1 == __n2
) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c"
, 1259, ((const char*) (__func__)), "decomp[2]" " " "==" " " "c"
, (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'x'); } while
(0); \

) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c"

(0); \

1350/* Test that g_unichar_decompose() whenever encouttering a char ch
1351 * decomposes into a and b, b itself won't decompose any further. */
1352static void
1353test_decompose_tail (void)
1354{
1355 gunichar ch, a, b, c, d;
1356
1357 /* Test that whenever a char ch decomposes into a and b, b itself
1358 * won't decompose any further. */
1359
1360 for (ch = 0; ch < 0x110000; ch++)
1361 if (g_unichar_decompose (ch, &a, &b))
1362 g_assert_false (g_unichar_decompose (b, &c, &d))do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (!(g_unichar_decompose (b, &c, &d))) _g_boolean_var_
= 1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else
g_assertion_message ("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 1362
, ((const char*) (__func__)), "'" "g_unichar_decompose (b, &c, &d)"
"' should be FALSE"); } while (0);
1363 else
1364 {
1365 g_assert_cmpuint (a, ==, ch)do { guint64 __n1 = (a), __n2 = (ch); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else
g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c"
, 1365, ((const char*) (__func__)), "a" " " "==" " " "ch", (long
double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0);
1366 g_assert_cmpuint (b, ==, 0)do { guint64 __n1 = (b), __n2 = (0); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else
g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c"
, 1366, ((const char*) (__func__)), "b" " " "==" " " "0", (long
double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0);
1367 }
1368}

1370/* Test that all canonical decompositions of g_unichar_fully_decompose()
1371 * are at most 4 in length, and compatibility decompositions are
1372 * at most 18 in length. */
1373static void
1374test_fully_decompose_len (void)
1375{
1376 gunichar ch;
1377
1378 /* Test that all canonical decompositions are at most 4 in length,
1379 * and compatibility decompositions are at most 18 in length.
1380 */
1381
1382 for (ch = 0; ch < 0x110000; ch++) {
1383 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_fully_decompose (ch, FALSE, NULL, 0), <=, 4)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_fully_decompose (ch, (0), ((void
*)0), 0)), __n2 = (4); if (__n1 <= __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum
("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 1383, ((const char*) (__func__
)), "g_unichar_fully_decompose (ch, FALSE, NULL, 0)" " " "<="
" " "4", (long double) __n1, "<=", (long double) __n2, 'i'
); } while (0);
1384 g_assert_cmpint (g_unichar_fully_decompose (ch, TRUE, NULL, 0), <=, 18)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_unichar_fully_decompose (ch, (!(0)), ((
void*)0), 0)), __n2 = (18); if (__n1 <= __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum
("GLib", "../glib/tests/unicode.c", 1384, ((const char*) (__func__
)), "g_unichar_fully_decompose (ch, TRUE, NULL, 0)" " " "<="
" " "18", (long double) __n1, "<=", (long double) __n2, 'i'
); } while (0);
1385 }
1386}
